Subject: [dm-l] CfP Materiality of Manuscripts - IMC 2023

Dear colleagues,

We are seeking papers dealing with manuscript studies for a series of sessions entitled Materiality of Manuscripts at the International Medieval Congress 2023.

We encourage comparative approaches and invite papers exploring especially the following topics:
·      networks of manuscript production, circulation and provenance
·      palaeographical and codicological approaches to manuscripts
·      digital approaches to researching manuscripts, including quantitative studies
·      teaching with manuscripts, including digital pedagogies

_redacted_(a)g_redacted_(a)gmail.com> by 25 September 2022, 23:59 CST.

With best wishes,

Kıvılcım & Katarzyna

Dr N. Kıvılcım Yavuz
Lecturer in Medieval Studies and Digital Humanities
Institute for Medieval Studies | School of History, University of Leeds

Dr Katarzyna Anna Kapitan
Junior Research Fellow, Linacre College, University of Oxford

[cid:039C60A6-892D-4808-9BE8-DD3CD3268C74]
